Grand Prix Trial Winning Decklists
==================================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on March 18, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_FrankKarsten.jpg)
By Frank Karsten











Yesterday, Grand Prix Shizuoka competitors had one last chance to earn two byes for the main event by entering the Grand Prix Trials. The winning decklists traditionally give a first impression of what to expect over the course of the weekend.


Below, you can find 21 decklists. The breakdown is as follows:


* 7 Mardu decks (2 with Veteran Motorist, 5 with just Walking Ballista)
* 6 Four-Color Saheeli decks (one with a delirium package)
* 3 Temur Aetherworks Marvel decks (one with Aetherwind Basker)
* 3 Black-Green decks (two Winding Constrictor variants, one energy variant)
* 1 Red-Black Eldrazi (featuring Ruins of Oran-Rief and Reality Smasher)
* 1 Jeskai Vehicles (so Spell Queller instead of Unlicensed Disintegration)
 




#### Hayakawa, Naoki (Mardu Vehicles)


##### 
 Grand Prix Shizuoka 2017 Spring LCT Winner






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
